Your Price $20.20 In Stock Add to cart Hedge Trimmer Tune-up Kit PartSelect Number PS11826164 Manufacturer Part Number 90152Y This tune-up kit is a genuine OEM replacement kit used in lawn and garden equipment. It is specially designed to provide you with everything you need to maintain your engine in one easy package. The kit includes one air filter, one spark plug, and one fuel filter. The air filter prevents contaminants in the air from flowing into the equipment engine. The fuel filter prevents contaminants from entering the fuel tank, and the spark plug is responsible for igniting the fuel and air mixture that allows the engine to run. It is normal for the filters to wear down or become clogged with debris over time while the spark plug can become fouled or damaged as well. If these parts are faulty, you will have difficulties starting your equipment, your engine may overheat and stall, and you will notice reduced power output from your equipment. It is recommended to replace these parts at the beginning of each season for optimal performance. Detach the air filter cover and clean the housing before placing the new air filter in place. Drain the fuel from the tank, disconnect the fuel lines, and replace the fuel filter. Finally, use a spark plug wrench to remove the faulty spark plug, and use a gaping tool to set the correct gap size on your new spark plug according to your model specifications. Thread the new spark plug in by hand and then tighten it with the wrench to complete your repair. Installation Instructions GARY from CARROLLTON, TX Annual tune up Tune up for blower, edger and string trimmer. Took 15 minutes to change 3 gas filters, air filters and spark plugs. Plugs had to be properly gapped. Read more... Your Price $17.95 In Stock Add to cart Vent Hood Light Switch ★★★★★ ★★★★★ 7 Reviews PartSelect Number PS953546 Manufacturer Part Number WB24X10130 This is the replacement light switch for your range. Fixes these symptoms Will Not Start See more... Installation Instructions Joseph from FLORENCE, NJ The plastic part of the switch that screws into the hex nut broke off. First, unplug the range hood, then remove the switch cover plate, held by two Phillips screws. Remove the switch knob and the hex nut on the front of the hood.(In my case, the hex nut had snapped off with the threaded part of the switch in it.) Then gently pull the switch away from the hood and write down which color wire (black, yellow, white) connects to which receptacle on the switch. The receptacles on the rear of the switch are marked L,1,2 and 3. 3 is left blank. Snip the wires from the switch, getting as close to the body of the switch as possible. Pulling them from the push-in receptacles doesn't work. Using a wire stripper, strip off about 1/2 inch of the wire insulation. Twist the exposed wires tightly and insert into the appropriate receptacles so that no bare wire shows. Insert the face of the switch into the hole on the hood so that the threaded portion protrudes. Using the hex nut provided, tighten snugly with an adjustable wrench. Do not over-tighten. Reattach the knob. Most of this repair went quickly and smoothly, but, despite repeated efforts, the threaded portion of the new switch did not fit through the original hole in the hood. As a result, I used a drill to enlarge the hole. The result was satisfactory but the new switch is not seated as well as the original. The knob does not line up exactly in the On, Off, Nite Light positions. Read more... Carbon brushes are wear items, meaning that through friction and use they will gradually wear away until they need replacing. Your Price $5.95 In Stock Add to cart Miter Saw Brush Box Asm PartSelect Number PS12522639 Manufacturer Part Number N292059 This is a brush box assembly designed for various sander models. Brush boxes are essential components that house carbon brushes responsible for transferring electricity from the motor to the sanding pad. When the carbon brush assembly wears out, it can no longer efficiently transfer electricity, causing the sander to stop working. This brush box assembly includes the carbon brush, its housing, and the necessary wiring. Replacing the brush box assembly is a straightforward process, requiring only a screwdriver and a set of pliers. Begin by disconnecting your sander from its power source, whether it is a battery or a wall outlet. Next, remove the screws securing the main housing of the sander and locate the brushes inside. Use a set of pliers to disconnect the wire from the old brush and a flat-head screwdriver to lift the old brush out of its slot. Insert the new brush box assembly into the slot and connect its wires. Finally, reattach the sander outer housing and secure it with the screws.
